< text>
North Star is a very great school. It provides a good environment for students to learn. Although people might have a few complaints, they are very lucky to attend such a terrific school. The school provides many extra curricular activities such as art programs, music programs and after school and lunch time clubs. In my experience students feel very safe and enjoy going here. Many people meet friends here that they will have for the rest of their lives. The teachers try their best to make learning fun and enjoyable for the students. There might be a lot of work and high exceptions sometimes but the teachers are just trying to better prepare you for the future. Teachers give the amount of homework that necessary for the class. Every student here should feel blessed to attend a school were teachers really want the best for their students.< /text>

<pics>None< /pics><Rating>5<//Rating><Name>Jill McHale<//Name>< Review>
We count our blessings every day that our kids were able to get into this unique school. We drive from San Mateo to attend, and it's worth it. After experiencing bullying, disruptive classes, and minimal oversight in public middle school with one child and teaching to the lowest common denominator in grade school for the other, it is so refreshing to attend North Star Academy.  The kids are unique and focused and the school caters to that kind of student. The principal sets the stage early, expectations are high, and the education is outstanding.  Another bonus is it's 3rd-8th grade so the "middle school shuffle" is non-existent.<//Review>

The middle school math program is bad, because everything is repetitive. There is an enrichment program with study hall, but the system for who goes into what enrichment is biased, so I often have to stay up very late to complete assignments. Also, the bathrooms are dirty. But it is also a good school. Many teachers are really nice. The learning environment is relaxing. There are many activities you can participate in, like music and enrichment. There is an art program where you learn about art. I have had a lot of fun at this school. We go on many fun field trips. <name>ConnorW8</name><time>1571461976945<//time><rating>5</rating>< review>
Class of 2019 (Connor Williams)

North Star Academy (NSA) is an amazing school and I went there from 3rd-8th grade. The community is very nice and all the teachers are very friendly and understanding. Principal Sara Shackel is an amazing principal, being both joyful and helping to improve the school. She has always listened to the emails I have sent complaining and offering suggestions about improving a specific situation at school, and does a great job dealing with conflicts between students.

The school stands out in may ways, including an enrichment program which starts in 4th grade, which is essentially an elective class. Some classes include going deep into math, composing music, learning to code, creating the yearbook (middle school), and helping run school events. This school helps ease the transition to middle school from it's rigorous elementary school curriculum, which is featured with learning all about fractions and negative numbers, doing the freedom project, and doing the science fair, with the latter two involving making a trifold. There are numerous field trips taken during the elementary grades, the most notable being the gold rush and outdoor ed field trips, which are 2 and 4 night field trips, respectively. These field trips are filled with excitement, adventure, and education. Middle school features the introduction of grades, more frequent essay writing, and the option to skip a grade in math (about 70% of students go this way). Additionally, you learn how to write stronger thesis essays, citing text for evidence, and get introductions to biology and physics. Along the way, you read many classics, including Bless me Ultima, To Kill a Mockingbird, and even a Shakespeare play. On top of all that, you do several projects, including dressing up as an Egyptian, designing a biosphere, learning about racial inequality, and using advanced math to design and create a 'doll' and make calculations on it. In middle school, there are also many notable field trips, including Marin Headlands, Yosemite, and DC/NYC (optional, over spring break), which happen in the 6th, 7th, and 8th grades, respectively.

All of these projects, activities, and field trips have well prepared me for high school, making it seem relatively easy compared to 8th grade at NSA. I have gotten so many opportunities over the year, including working on the yearbook, flying a drone, and helping transform our news program, KNSA. Yes, I edited all the KNSA videos in the 2018-19 school year. The photo in the front cover of the 2019 yearbook was shot by me. I miss going to this school, but I still visit once in a while to say hi to all the teachers and students I have left to go to high school.</review>

< Review>
I was getting really tired of overpaying for subpar service and shotty reception with ATT after being with them for over 10 years. I finally decided to make the switch based on the testament from family and friends I would get a much better value for my money with Verizon. I came in to port my number and luckily there was no wait. The last time I had step foot in an ATT store a few days ago I was 12th in line with an estimated wait time of 2 HOURS!!!

Kim, the associate that I had the pleasure of working with was super friendly and personable, she truly made the switch effortless. Answered all my questions and I was in my new iPhone 7+ in no time! I was impressed by the above and beyond treatment I received here.

The Verizon network does not disappoint, my LTE is light years faster and more reliable than what I have been experiencing with my old service provider and have full bars! Really glad I made the switch and wish I had done it sooner.< /Review>

< review>
After calling around to many storage companies in the Palm Desert area, it was clear that Life Storage was our choice!  Beau, at the front desk took my call and helped us secure our storage unit.  He's knowledgeable, was very patient with all our questions, and has a good sense of humor.  Both Beau and Matt continue to provide terrific customer service whenever we call in, including the day On Time Storage (also awesome!) delivered our home goods.  Beau took us on his golf cart to show us the unit, making sure the size would fit our belongings.  What we LOVE about this storage company is that there are NO elevators, which can greatly increase the moving time and expense when bringing items in and out of the storage unit.  All second level units are simply accessed by driving up to that level.  Besides great pricing, the hours that people have access to their units is much longer than most other companies.  Thank you again to both Beau and Matt!</review>

I am stunned that a company would treat customers that experienced a unit break-in at their facility - caused by their poor security practices -  this poorly, but here we are.

When we called the facility we spoke with Beaux and were told our storage unit had been broken into. We informed him that we were on vacation and couldn't do anything but would handle it as soon as we were back in town. After that conversation it was assumed that everything was good, but when we came home and went to look in on the storage unit we found out two very surprising things.

1) When we got to the office we were told that the facility staff member had let the burglar in because he said "I forgot my code". The facility let the thief in without checking his ID or anything - just buzzed him right in.

Beaux was clearly pissed that he had to deal with it and took it out on us. After going to look at our unit door, the only part that was broken was the latch that allows someone to use a personal lock. It was basically ripped off, meaning it wasn't the padlock that allowed the robber in, so the type of lock would have made zero difference.

Beaux then said he would give us the lock 50% off but he would "catch hell" for doing that, giving us grief the whole time. We again said we didn't want the lock. Beaux then told us that he wouldn't fix the door or give us another unit. We were basically now forced to buy his lock. So we purchased the lock and secured our unit so we could get out.

It's ridiculous that someone who let in the individual who broke in to our unit would then harass, take advantage and force us to buy one of his products. There was zero remorse or empathy from this man. Maybe he was having a bad day, but he should never have taken that out on us. We were in a vulnerable position and Beaux did absolutely nothing to help. Shame on you and shame on your company. Life Storage, you really need to re-evaluate who you allow to run your facilities. We'll be taking our business to Security Public Storage on the other side of the freeway.</text>

<Text>My experience was good overall.  It was easy to check-in and complete the paperwork, the car was very nice and clean, and the (online) rate was exceptional.  However, there were a couple of items that bothered me.

First, it was a little confusing to find out where to leave the car when returning.

Next, there is a sign at the counter saying if you drive less than 75 miles to not fill up the car and they'll take care of it ... for $13.99.  I didn't want this option, so I filled up the car myself (for $8), but the $13.99 was still charged to my card and I had indicated on the folder upon return that I had filled the car.  My mistake, and it was only $14, but...

Lastly, keep in mind that if you get a special online rate (mine was $34 for 2 days) and you have an interest in keeping it another day, make sure you ask what the cost is BEFORE you close out your contract.  Once they close it out, they cannot (or so my agent said) reopen it.  Thus, had I wanted to keep it another day, if I asked before I closed it out, the cost would have been $17.  After it became over $100.</Text>< Pictures>
